[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-text-m[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/csv/CellFormatter.jav[0m[1;92ma:40[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m47[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:    String [0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcell == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:            cell = [0m[32m""[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:        String trimmedCell = [0m[1;35mcell.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mfractionFormatMatcher.reset[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrimmedCell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mfractionFormatMatcher.matches[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:            return cell;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The hanging occurs in [0m[1;35mCellFormatter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m’s nested brute-force loops [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m75[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The outer loop runs i from [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength–[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m down to [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, and the inner loop runs[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mi2 from [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength–[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m down to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since the regex allows denomFormat lengths up to [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m characters, this becomes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m × [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m iterations for a pathological input, causing a CPU-bound hang.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Overview  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce a safe upper bound on `[0m[1;35mdenomFormat.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before entering the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrute-force approximation.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the requested denominator format is too large [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., > [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, skip the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpensive search and return the original cell string unmodified.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This preserves existing functionality for reasonable fraction formats while [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotecting against fuzzed or malicious inputs that would trigger combinatorial [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblow-up.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps to Implement the Patch  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `CellFormatter.java`, add a new constant at class scope:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Maximum number of digits in denominator to attempt brute-force [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproximation[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final int MAX_DENOM_LENGTH = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In the `[0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, immediately after the regex match check [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand before parsing group values, insert:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String denomFormat = [0m[1;35mfractionFormatMatcher.group[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mdenomFormat.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > MAX_DENOM_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Skip expensive approximation for overly large formats[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return cell;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Move on to parse `val`, compute `wholeFormat`, `numFormat`, and proceed into [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe loops only when `[0m[1;35mdenomFormat.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is within the safe bound.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Ensure imports and class-level declarations remain unchanged, and that no [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother logic in `[0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is altered.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification & Preservation of Logic  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By returning the original cell for large `denomFormat`, we avoid CPU [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion while still allowing the CSV parser to continue.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Legitimate use cases—where `[0m[1;35mdenomFormat.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is ≤ [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m—are unaffected, so [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests and functionality pass unchanged.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This guard complements the existing regex [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich already limits [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumerator/denominator format strings to ≤ [0m[1;36m20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but applies a practical runtime [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbound.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rarely, a user might request a denominator with more than [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m digits to achieve [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhigher-precision formatting. In such a case, the cell is returned unformatted.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - To mitigate confusion, document this behavior in the Javadoc for [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mCellFormatter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, so users understand that extremely large formats are [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbypassed.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If finer approximation for large formats is ever required, consider [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementing a continued-fraction algorithm rather than brute force.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. No Changes to Harness or Tests  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix does not modify any fuzzing harness, external libraries, or test code.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests that supply reasonable fraction formats continue to succeed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout alteration.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy adding this simple guard, we prevent the exponential inner loops from hanging [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe parser under fuzzed inputs, thus resolving the libFuzzer timeout issue while [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving CSV parsing semantics for typical use cases.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
